< Review>
Hope this place does well. Basically a newer, smaller, even more casual version of Bar Ama in downtown. Wouldn‚Äôt say the queso was as good as the one I had at Bar Ama, but it‚Äôs been a while and I still recommend getting it and adding more chips to eat it with. Really like the idea of the bigger format meat dishes to eat with handmade flour tortillas. Got the Denver steak and one of the roast chickens (Mexican marinated one) and while they were cooked well, it came out just a little cold. They could maybe be sliced better so you can fill up the tacos more easily. Service was just a little slow but overall I really like the concept. Also recommend the homemade craft sodas, those were cool. Pricing is really solid.<//Review>

< text>
For a couple of years, this was the Baco Shop, a fast casual place with good food. Now, the owners have reconfigured it as a sit-down Tex-Mex restaurant and bar. There is a similar place downtown, Bar Ama. The food is good. Delicious flour tortillas are featured in many dishes. Queso was well garnished, and a summer salad with peach and tomato was delicious. Pork shoulder pibil was very good, served with three puffy & yummy flour tortillas.<//text>

<UserId.>108400556566101213242<//UserId.><user_name>Lorrin Wong<//user_name>< date>

<Review>We know Josef Centeno from Orsa & Winston in downtown and the earlier Baco Shop which was in this location. While we were saddened that Baco Shop closed, we're more than happy with the change to Ama-cita (Tex-Mex). This was a wonderful find and much closer to our home. We've eaten there multiple times since their opening a few weeks ago.

The menu is tapas style and intended to be shared. There are a number of vegetarian and vegan choices so my wife doesn't go away hungry. But there are meat dishes, like carne guisado (braised marinated beef), to satisfy the carnivores. There is a nice balance between innovation and tradition. Food is delicious. Don't look for tacos or enchiladas. It's Tex-Mex, not Mexican.

Rather modest wine and beer list until they get their liquor license. Staff is friendly, cheerful and helpful. They may still be working out some of the opening day kinks but if Josef's other restaurants are a guide, Ama-cita will operate in tip top shape shortly.

There is a limited amount of patio (street side) dining. I don't know if they take reservations. We've come on the spur of the moment but the restaurant is already popular and can be crowded.

Parking is a problem, particularly for handicapped people. There are city parking structures a few blocks away for those who are mobile. We use Lyft.< /Review>< pictures>

< Text>
As a heads up to those customers that have sports cars, you might want to choose another dealer to service your vehicle.

I had my son's Sonic serviced at Silverstar and they did a good job, oil was changed, tires rotated, car washed and ready when promised.

I figured I'd have my G8GT serviced there, and that is when it went off the rails.  They did service the car, however the car was abused while entrusted to the dealer.  The car had been driven hard, with significant tire residue left over from burnouts on the front of the mufflers.  The guilty party tried to cover their tracks by washing the rear wheel wells and zeroing out both the trip odometer and the MPG average.  However, they forgot about the undercarriage.

Additionally, I had a brand new scratch on the drivers side of the car that I had to buff out.

To add insult to injury, they told me that my rear tire wear was low...on one year old tires.  I figure the check was done after all the burnouts.

If you have an economy focused car I think you are safe with this dealer doing your service.  If you have a performance car, I'd shy away.  I know that I won't be back.</Text>

< Review>
They are always very fast which is one of the big pluses that I like about going there. It's better to make an appointment ahead of time because if they're really busy you show up they might not get to you fast enough.

normally I would put five stars, but the prices have gone up and instead of the company incurring fees for washing the cars they have now added that to the consumer.
